<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:интеллигенция.html>интеллиге́нция</a> (3214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">intellegentia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">intelligence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интеллигенция.html>интеллиге́нция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">intelligéncija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интеллигенция.html>интеллиге́нции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интеллигенция.html>интеллиге́нции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интеллигенция.html>интеллиге́нций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>intelligentsia, the intellectuals collectively</li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">«Я отлично знаю, ― говорит он [Леонардо да Винчи], ― что так как я неучёный человек (non essere io letterato), то некоторым заносчивым людям может казаться, что они вправе порицать меня, говоря, что я лишён образования (essere io uomo senza lettere). Глупцы! Не знают они, что я могу ответить им, как Марий отвечал римским патрициям: они сделали себе украшение из чужих трудов, а за мною не хотят признать моих собственных!» Этими словами Леонардо очень точно выразил мысль, вполне характеризовавшую его положение в обществе: он не гуманист (в XV веке — последователь мистико-религиозной философии), но он принадлежит к <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">интеллигенции</span>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:собирательный.html>собира́тельное</a>">собир.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:разговорный.html>разгово́рное</a>">разг.</span> люди, принадлежащие к этой группе, лица умственного труда, интеллигенты <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Видимо, нас считали местной <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">интеллигенцией</span>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>
</body>

***интенсивно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:интенсивный.html>интенси́вно</a> (19156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интенсивный.html>интенси́вный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">intɛnsívnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интенсивный.html>интенси́вно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">intɛnsívno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>intensively</li>
<li>vigorously</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***интерес.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́с</a> (657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">interés</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>interest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вас</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto iméjet <b>interés</b> dlja vas.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This is of interest to you.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́сах</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>interésax</b> míra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the interest of peace</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>interés</b> k</i> ― <span class="e-translation">interest in (+ dative)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***интересно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a> (893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересный.html>интере́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">interésnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">interésno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-интере́сно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)интере́снее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-интере́сно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)интере́сней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>interestingly, in an interesting manner
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассказывать.html>расска́зывает</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>interésno</b> rasskázyvajet.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">His way of retelling is quite interesting.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">He retells interestingly.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">interésno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>it is interesting <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne óčenʹ <b>interésno</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It's very interesting (to me).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>I wonder <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">introduces a clause</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:куда.html>куда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делиться.html>де́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Interésno</b>, kudá délisʹ moí očkí?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I wonder where my glasses are gone to?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">interésno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересный.html>интере́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">interésnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:произведение.html>произведе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:довольно.html>дово́льно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto proizvedénije dovólʹno <b>interésno</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">This (literary) work is rather interesting.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***интернет.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́т</a> (5847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Internet</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">intɛrnɛ́t</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>the Internet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вчера.html>вчера́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́те</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Skólʹko vy včerá sidéli v <b>intɛrnɛ́te</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">How long did you hang out on the <b>internet</b> yesterday?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The plural form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́ты</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">intɛrnɛ́ty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used in a humorous way, like internets (from G. W. Bush).
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:интимный.html>интимно</a> (29318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:интриговать.html>интригова́ть</a> (25736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интрига.html>интри́га</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">intríga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интриговать.html>интригова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">intrigovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заинтриговать.html>заинтригова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to plot, to scheme</li>
<li>to intrigue, to interest greatly</li></ol>
